following major components:\\n\\n## 1. Event Creation and Entry Point\\n**EventTarget::DispatchEvent** (dom/events/EventTarget.cpp:212-222)\\n- Public API for dispatching events on any DOM element\\n- Overloaded versions accept Event references and ErrorResult\\n- Delegates to EventDispatcher::Dispatch for actual dispatching\\n\\n## 2. Event Target Chain Construction\\n**EventDispatcher::Dispatch** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:869-1360)\\n- Main event dispatching orchestrator\\n- Creates the event target chain by calling GetEventTargetParent on each target\\n- Initializes EventChainPreVisitor to track pre-dispatch state\\n- Builds chain upward from initial target through parents until no more parents exist\\n- Handles event retargeting for Shadow DOM and anonymous content\\n\\n**EventTargetChainItem** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.h/cpp)\\n- Represents individual items in the event target chain\\n- Contains methods:\\n  - GetEventTargetParent: Builds chain by calling target's GetEventTargetParent method\\n  - PreHandleEvent: Called before event listener invocation\\n  - PostHandleEvent: Called after event listener invocation  \\n  - HandleEvent: Invokes event listeners via EventListenerManager\\n  - ActivationBehavior: Executes default actions\\n\\n## 3. Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal\\n**HandleEventTargetChain** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:480-694)\\n- Traverses the event target chain for capture, target, and bubble phases\\n- Handles two event groups: default group and system group\\n\\nPhase execution order:\\n1. **Capture Phase** (lines 519-540): Iterates chain from root to target\\n   - Sets mInCapturePhase flag\\n   - Invokes listeners registered with capture=true\\n   - Calls PostHandleEvent for each target in system group\\n\\n2. **Target Phase** (lines 587-611): At the original event target\\n   - Sets mInTargetPhase flag\\n   - Invokes both capture and non-capture listeners\\n   - Calls PostHandleEvent\\n\\n3. **Bubble Phase** (lines 613-648): Iterates chain from target to root\\n   - Sets mInBubblingPhase flag\\n   - Invokes listeners registered with capture=false (if event bubbles)\\n   - Calls PostHandleEvent for each target in system group\\n\\n4. **System Event Group** (lines 651-693): Repeats phases for system listeners\\n   - Resets propagation flags\\n   - Re-dispatches to system event group listeners\\n   - Allows default action execution\\n\\n## 4. Event Listener Invocation\\n**EventListenerManager::HandleEventSingleListener** (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1233-1310)\\n- Invokes a single event listener on the current event target\\n- Steps:\\n  1. Sets event.currentTarget to the current target (line 1237)\\n  2. Marks if listener is passive (line 1243)\\n  3. Stores previous window event for proper scoping\\n  4. Compiles event handler if it's a string (lines 1261-1262)\\n  5. Calls listener.HandleEvent with EventTarget and Event (line 1276)\\n  6. Default Action Execution\\n\\n**PreHandleEvent** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:455-458)\\n- Called BEFORE event listeners are invoked\\n- Allows targets to perform preparatory actions\\n- Can set flags to influence listener invocation\\n- Called during the pre-dispatch phase (EventDispatcher::Dispatch lines 1077-1078, 1200)\\n\\n**PostHandleEvent** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:483-524)\\n- Called AFTER event listeners are invoked for each target\\n- Called only in system event group dispatch (lines 609, 645)\\n- Updates visitor with target's item flags and data\\n- Can modify event handling based on listener results\\n\\n**ActivationBehavior** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp)\\n- Executes default action for activation events (click, etc.)\\n- Called after event dispatch completes if:\\n  - Event wasn't preventDefault'd (line 1340)\\n  - Target was marked as activation target during dispatch\\n- Implementations in specific elements (HTMLButtonElement, HTMLInputElement, etc.)\\n\\n## 6. Event Flow Control\\n\\nThe dispatch process manages several flags in the event:\\n- mInCapturePhase: Currently in capture phase\\n- mInTargetPhase: Currently at the target\\n- mInBubblingPhase: Currently in bubble phase\\n- mPropagationStopped: stopPropagation() was called\\n- mImmediatePropagationStopped: stopImmediatePropagation() was called\\n- mDefaultPrevented: preventDefault() was called\\n\\nListeners can be configured as:\\n- Capturing (capture=true) - fires in capture phase\\n- Bubbling (capture=false) - fires in bubble phase and target phase\\n- Passive - cannot call preventDefault()\\n- Once - automatically removed after first invocation\\n\\n## 7. Shadow DOM and Retargeting\\n\\nThe event system handles:\\n- Event retargeting across shadow boundaries (EventChainPreVisitor lines 137-140)\\n- Composed path calculation considering shadow trees\\n- Target adjustment based on shadow tree composition\\n- Anonymous content retargeting\\n\\n## 8. Key Data Structures\\n\\n**EventChainVisitor** (EventDispatcher.h:53-111)\\n- Base visitor for event chain traversal\\n- Contains: presContext, event, mDOMEvent, eventStatus, itemFlags, itemData\\n\\n**EventChainPreVisitor** (EventDispatcher.h:113-260)\\n- Extends EventChainVisitor with pre-dispatch state\\n- Tracks: canHandle, automaticChromeDispatch, retargeted targets, parent targets\\n\\n**EventChainPostVisitor** (EventDispatcher.h:318-330)\\n- Extends EventChainVisitor for post-dispatch operations\\n- Used after event listener invocation\\n- Carries PostHandleEvent results\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe complete event dispatch flow is:\\n\\n1. EventTarget::DispatchEvent → EventDispatcher::Dispatch (creates chain)\\n2. Build event target chain via GetEventTargetParent (up to document/window)\\n3. Call PreHandleEvent on all targets (setup phase)\\n4. HandleEventTargetChain iterates:\\n   - Capture phase: root → target, invoke capture listeners\\n   - Target phase: invoke all listeners on original target\\n   - Bubble phase: target → root, invoke bubble listeners\\n5. PostHandleEvent called after listeners (post-processing)\\n6. Default group dispatch completes\\n7. System group dispatch with same phases\\n8. ActivationBehavior executed if not prevented (default action)\\n\\nThis design separates concerns between event routing, listener management, and default action handling, allowing flexible event processing in Firefox's DOM implementation.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2342,"cache_read_input_tokens":89833,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2342},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"cd05a8f2-4fed-40f7-b64f-e190b9dcfaaa","uuid":"19023665-0353-4a8c-a8c7-e48445ac9c00"}

Chain Implementation\\n\\n## Overview\\nThe Firefox event dispatch system is implemented in the dom/events directory with the following major components:\\n\\n## 1. Event Creation and Entry Point\\n**EventTarget::DispatchEvent** (dom/events/EventTarget.cpp:212-222)\\n- Public API for dispatching events on any DOM element\\n- Overloaded versions accept Event references and ErrorResult\\n- Delegates to EventDispatcher::Dispatch for actual dispatching\\n\\n## 2. Event Target Chain Construction\\n**EventDispatcher::Dispatch** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:869-1360)\\n- Main event dispatching orchestrator\\n- Creates the event target chain by calling GetEventTargetParent on each target\\n- Initializes EventChainPreVisitor to track pre-dispatch state\\n- Builds chain upward from initial target through parents until no more parents exist\\n- Handles event retargeting for Shadow DOM and anonymous content\\n\\n**EventTargetChainItem** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.h/cpp)\\n- Represents individual items in the event target chain\\n- Contains methods:\\n  - GetEventTargetParent: Builds chain by calling target's GetEventTargetParent method\\n  - PreHandleEvent: Called before event listener invocation\\n  - PostHandleEvent: Called after event listener invocation  \\n  - HandleEvent: Invokes event listeners via EventListenerManager\\n  - ActivationBehavior: Executes default actions\\n\\n## 3. Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal\\n**HandleEventTargetChain** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:480-694)\\n- Traverses the event target chain for capture, target, and bubble phases\\n- Handles two event groups: default group and system group\\n\\nPhase execution order:\\n1. **Capture Phase** (lines 519-540): Iterates chain from root to target\\n   - Sets mInCapturePhase flag\\n   - Invokes listeners registered with capture=true\\n   - Calls PostHandleEvent for each target in system group\\n\\n2. **Target Phase** (lines 587-611): At the original event target\\n   - Sets mInTargetPhase flag\\n   - Invokes both capture and non-capture listeners\\n   - Calls PostHandleEvent\\n\\n3. **Bubble Phase** (lines 613-648): Iterates chain from target to root\\n   - Sets mInBubblingPhase flag\\n   - Invokes listeners registered with capture=false (if event bubbles)\\n   - Calls PostHandleEvent for each target in system group\\n\\n4. **System Event Group** (lines 651-693): Repeats phases for system listeners\\n   - Resets propagation flags\\n   - Re-dispatches to system event group listeners\\n   - Allows default action execution\\n\\n## 4. Event Listener Invocation\\n**EventListenerManager::HandleEventSingleListener** (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1233-1310)\\n- Invokes a single event listener on the current event target\\n- Steps:\\n  1. Sets event.currentTarget to the current target (line 1237)\\n  2. Marks if listener is passive (line 1243)\\n  3. Stores previous window event for proper scoping\\n  4. Compiles event handler if it's a string (lines 1261-1262)\\n  5. Calls listener.HandleEvent with EventTarget and Event (line 1276)\\n  6. Returns false if propagation stopped or immediate propagation stopped\\n\\n**EventListenerManager::HandleEventWithListenerArray** (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1536-1627)\\n- Iterates through all listeners for an event type\\n- Filters by event phase (capture vs bubble)\\n- Handles 'once' listeners by removing them during dispatch\\n- Ensures DOM event is lazily created when first listener is invoked\\n\\n**EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:339-375)\\n- Called for each item in the chain during appropriate phase\\n- Gets or creates EventListenerManager for the target\\n- Invokes EventListenerManager::HandleEvent to fire all listeners for this event type\\n\\n## 5. Default Action Execution\\n\\n**PreHandleEvent** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:455-458)\\n- Called BEFORE event listeners are invoked\\n- Allows targets to perform preparatory actions\\n- Can set flags to influence listener invocation\\n- Called during the pre-dispatch phase (EventDispatcher::Dispatch lines 1077-1078, 1200)\\n\\n**PostHandleEvent** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:483-524)\\n- Called AFTER event listeners are invoked for each target\\n- Called only in system event group dispatch (lines 609, 645)\\n- Updates visitor with target's item flags and data\\n- Can modify event handling based on listener results\\n\\n**ActivationBehavior** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp)\\n- Executes default action for activation events (click, etc.)\\n- Called after event dispatch completes if:\\n  - Event wasn't preventDefault'd (line 1340)\\n  - Target was marked as activation target during dispatch\\n- Implementations in specific elements (HTMLButtonElement, HTMLInputElement, etc.)\\n\\n## 6. Event Flow Control\\n\\nThe dispatch process manages several flags in the event:\\n- mInCapturePhase: Currently in capture phase\\n- mInTargetPhase: Currently at the target\\n- mInBubblingPhase: Currently in bubble phase\\n- mPropagationStopped: stopPropagation() was called\\n- mImmediatePropagationStopped: stopImmediatePropagation() was called\\n- mDefaultPrevented: preventDefault() was called\\n\\nListeners can be configured as:\\n- Capturing (capture=true) - fires in capture phase\\n- Bubbling (capture=false) - fires in bubble phase and target phase\\n- Passive - cannot call preventDefault()\\n- Once - automatically removed after first invocation\\n\\n## 7. Shadow DOM and Retargeting\\n\\nThe event system handles:\\n- Event retargeting across shadow boundaries (EventChainPreVisitor lines 137-140)\\n- Composed path calculation considering shadow trees\\n- Target adjustment based on shadow tree composition\\n- Anonymous content retargeting\\n\\n## 8. Key Data Structures\\n\\n**EventChainVisitor** (EventDispatcher.h:53-111)\\n- Base visitor for event chain traversal\\n- Contains: presContext, event, mDOMEvent, eventStatus, itemFlags, itemData\\n\\n**EventChainPreVisitor** (EventDispatcher.h:113-260)\\n- Extends EventChainVisitor with pre-dispatch state\\n- Tracks: canHandle, automaticChromeDispatch, retargeted targets, parent targets\\n\\n**EventChainPostVisitor** (EventDispatcher.h:318-330)\\n- Extends EventChainVisitor for post-dispatch operations\\n- Used after event listener invocation\\n- Carries PostHandleEvent results\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe complete event dispatch flow is:\\n\\n1. EventTarget::DispatchEvent → EventDispatcher::Dispatch (creates chain)\\n2. Build event target chain via GetEventTargetParent (up to document/window)\\n3. Call PreHandleEvent on all targets (setup phase)\\n4. HandleEventTargetChain iterates:\\n   - Capture phase: root → target, invoke capture listeners\\n   - Target phase: invoke all listeners on original target\\n   - Bubble phase: target → root, invoke bubble listeners\\n5. PostHandleEvent called after listeners (post-processing)\\n6. Default group dispatch completes\\n7. System group dispatch with same phases\\n8. ActivationBehavior executed if not prevented (default action)\\n\\nThis design separates concerns between event routing, listener management, and default action handling, allowing flexible event processing in Firefox's DOM implementation.\"\n    43→}\n    44→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
